CASCADE;\n\n-- Vendors table\nCREATE TABLE vendors (\n    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,\n    vendor_id VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    phone VARCHAR(20),\n    company_name VARCHAR(255),\n    profile TEXT,\n    beautified_profile TEXT,\n    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'active',\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Catalogs table (uploaded PDF/Excel files)\nCREATE TABLE catalogs (\n    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,\n    catalog_id VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    vendor_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES vendors(vendor_id),\n    original_filename VARCHAR(255),\n    file_type VARCHAR(20),\n    file_size INTEGER,\n    total_pages INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    total_images INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    total_tables INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    total_products INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'processing',\n    minio_path VARCHAR(500),\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    processed_at TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Products table\nCREATE TABLE products (\n    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,\n    product_id VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    vendor_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES vendors(vendor_id),\n    catalog_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES catalogs(catalog_id),\n    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,\n    description TEXT,\n    price DECIMAL(10,2),\n    category VARCHAR(100),\n    subcategory VARCHAR(100),\n    sku VARCHAR(100),\n CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Product images table\nCREATE TABLE product_images (\n    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,\n    image_id VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    product_id VARCHAR(50) REFERENCES minio_bucket VARCHAR(100),\n    minio_path VARCHAR(500),\n    minio_url VARCHAR(1000),\n    thumbnail_url VARCHAR(1000),\n    width INTEGER,\n    height INTEGER,\n    file_size INTEGER,\n    mime_type VARCHAR(50),\n    is_primary BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    extracted_text TEXT,\n    ai_tags TEXT[],\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Notifications table\nCREATE TABLE notifications (\n    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,\n    notification_id VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    vendor_id VARCHAR(50),\n    type VARCHAR(50),\n    title VARCHAR(255),\n    message TEXT,\n    data JSONB,\n    read BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Create indexes for faster queries\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_vendor ON products(vendor_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_category ON products(category);\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_catalog ON products(catalog_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_images_product ON product_images(product_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_images_catalog ON product_images(catalog_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_catalogs_vendor ON catalogs(vendor_id);\n\n-- Insert sample data to verify\nINSERT INTO (text || '').toLowerCase();\n  for (const [category, keywords] of Object.entries(CATEGORIES)) {\n    if (keywords.some(kw => lowerText.includes(kw))) {\n      return category;\n    }\n  }\n  return 'general';\n}\n\n// Extract price from text\nfunction extractPrice(text) {\n  const priceMatch = text.match(/\\$\\s*(\\d{1,3}(?:,\\d{3})*(?:\\.\\d{2})?)/);\n  if (priceMatch) {\n    return parseFloat(priceMatch[1].replace(/,/g, ''));\n  }\n  const numMatch = text.match(/(\\d{1,3}(?:,\\d{3})*(?:\\.\\d{2})?)\\s*(?:USD|dollars?)/i);\n  if (numMatch) {\n    return pdfParse(dataBuffer);\n      stats.totalPages = pdfData.numpages;\n      console.log(`[PDF] Pages: ${stats.totalPages}, Text length: ${pdfData.text.length}`);\n    }\n    \n    // Extract images using try {\n        const opts = {\n          format: 'png',\n          out_dir: outputDir,\n          out_prefix: 'page',\n          scale: 1024\n        };\n        \n        await pdfPoppler.convert(filePath, opts);\n        console.log(`[PDF] Converted pages to images in ${outputDir}`);\n        \n        // Process each page image\n        const pageFiles = fs.readdirSync(outputDir).filter(f => f.endsWith('.png')).sort();\n        \n        for (let i = 0; i < pageFiles.length; i++) {\n          const pageFile = pageFiles[i];\n          const pagePath =        const imageBuffer = fs.readFileSync(pagePath);\n          const metadata = await sharp(imageBuffer).metadata();\n          \n          // Upload full image to MinIO\n          const imageResult minio.uploadThumbnail(\n            vendorId, catalogId, pageNum, 1, thumbBuffer\n          );\n          \n          stats.totalImages++;\n          \n          // Create product for this page\n db.createProduct({\n            productId,\n            vendorId,\n            catalogId,\n            name: `${vendorName} Product - Page ${pageNum}`,\n            description: pageText.slice(0, 500) inStock: true,\n            sourcePage: pageNum,\n            aiEnhanced: true,\n            aiDescription: `AI-enhanced product from ${vendorName}. vendorId,\n            originalPage: pageNum,\n            imageIndex: 1,\n            minioBucket: imageResult.bucket,\n            minioPath: imageResult.path,\n            minioUrl: \n    // Update catalog stats\n    await db.updateCatalogStats(catalogId, stats);\n    \n    return { products, images, stats };\n    \n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('[PDF] Processing const linesPerPage = Math.ceil(lines.length / totalPages);\n  const startLine = (pageNum - 1) * linesPerPage;\n  const endLine = pageNum * linesPerPage;\n  return lines.slice(startLine, endLine).join(' ').trim();\n}\n\n// Fallback: create products from text when images can't be extracted\nasync function createProductsFromText(pdfData, vendorId, catalogId, vendorName, products, stats) {\n  if (!pdfData || !pdfData.text) return;\n  \n  const text = pdfData.text;\n  const lines = text.split('\\n').filter(l => l.trim().length > 10);\n  \n  // Find product-like entries (lines with    products.push(product);\n      productCount++;\n      stats.totalProducts++;\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // If no products found, create some based on vendor name\n  if (productCount === 0) {\n    for (let stats.totalTables = Math.min(3, Math.floor(stats.totalProducts / 3));\n}\n\n// Process Excel file\nasync function processExcel(filePath, vendorId, catalogId, vendorName) {\n  console.log(`[Excel] 0) || \n                    (99 + Math.random() * 400);\n      const description = row.Description || row.description || row.Details || row.details || \n                          `Product from ${minioResult.path}`);\n    \n    // Process the file\n    let result;\n    if (fileExt === '.pdf') {\n      result = await pdfProcessor.processPDF(filePath, vendorId, catalogId, vendorName);\n    }
